Parthenopeius

Paruum doctrinale

→ Alanus ab Insula

Paruum uolumen, a standard collection

: pr. Mainz 1477 &c.; ed. A. & M. Kriegel, Corpus iuris ciuilis (Leipzig 1866). Its contents comprised Books X–XII of Justinian's Codex (known as the Tres libri); Justinian's Nouellae; Libri feudorum; Tractatus de pace Constantiae; Extrauagantes duae Henrici VII imperatoris; and Constitutiones Frederici II imperatoris. [The Paruum uolumen is often paired with Justinian's Institutiones.]
